"Men will always he what women make them: 
If, therefore, you would have men great and virtuous, impress upon the minds of women what greatness and virtue are." 
ROSSEAU. 
ISISHA YELELO. 
   Lencwajana ehalwe nguMnu. Johannes 2ama iyisifnndiso kwaliadaIa. naliancane ukulia ahadala hakhulise kahle izingane zaho, nezingane zikhule kahle ngokulalela imfundiso enhle yaliazali liazo. 
   Knlezizinsuku lapho aliazali Heyekethise imfundiso yezingane, iyolukhulu usizo. Kxa ngiyifiuku, iqondene naliazali naliantwana, kulaHo aliathanda inzalo yalio ikhnle ngoliuqotho. 
   UZama uyaqalisa ukuhala, kepha indlela ahala Ilgayo ayejwayclekile, nokho ibonisa isitno sCluiqondo yalezizinsuku. Bayoshesha ulullnuzwa alialezizikhathi. 
   Ngethemha amakholwa ayoyifundisisa, ifanekisa impatho yaliantwana ngaliazali, aliantwana liakhule ngemfanelo.

J. L. DUBE.
